< Review>
I hate to do this, but I had a rather terrible experience with them recently. This is aimed more at the staff out front than the actual optometrists, because they're both fantastic! So I had found their website (which one of them claims doesn't exist) and I went ahead and asked for an appointment. They promptly e-mailed me back with an available time and I agreed to it. I showed up at my appointment time and let the man know I was there for it, and he proceeds to tell me that I didn't make an appointment. So I inform him that I did, and tell him I made the appointment online. Nope, nothing. I'm furious at this point because I had been in dire need of new glasses (See my other review about Woori Optical) and I come to find out that I have no appointment and the person behind the desk has no idea that they even had a website. So he gives me an appointment at a later time that day, and I've settled down a bit, and I leave. That was the worst experience I've had there. The rest of the staff out front can be rude and give off an attitude, though, so just a warning.

The doctors themselves are both wonderful women, and are very attentive and make sure to ask a lot of questions. They remember who you are and even things you've told them, which is really great, it just shows they care.

I just implore the both of them to get better staff, I understand why this wouldn't be considered, but when you have employees who don't even know you have a website, where you take appointment requests over E-mail that goes to you, and the other two have a tendency to be extremely rude to patients who may not be able to articulate themselves better due to a language barrier, something must be done about it.<//Review>

< Rating>
5< /Rating>
<text>Can a pub get 10 stars? Can anything get 10 Stars? We visited this place while roaming around wine country. First off it's a Cheers type bar with a loyal local clientele as well as tourists. They specialize in handcrafted drinks with hard to find spirits. There is an eclectic menu that changes almost daily and good for quick bites. Diavalo's Pizza next door is owned by the same chef and we ordered gnocchi from their menu and ate at the gun club bar. I've eaten hundreds of gnocchi dishes and this was by far and away the most unusual, and almost risky recipe, so much so that I just had to try it. It was the bomb!    I wanted to live in Geyserville just so I could hang out and eat there. If you are in the area and tired of high-priced meals, this is just the place to eat well, at a moderate price.</text>< Pictures>
None</Pictures>
